## Instruction

Please read the table titled "GDP2022" in Google Sheets and calculate the CR5 index for each of the seven major regions listed by the World Bank. Create a new spreadsheet in Google Sheets, name it "GDP CR5 Analysis", and within it, create a new table titled "gdp_cr5_analysis". Save the following data: `Region`, `Top5_Countries`, `Top5_GDP_Sum`, `Region_GDP_Total`, and `CR5_Ratio`, where they represent the region name, the top five countries (separated by commas), the sum of the top five countries' GDP, the total regional GDP, and the CR5 index (percentage, rounded to two decimal places). Sort the data in descending order by CR5 index. (If you're unsure which region the World Bank assigns a country to, you can search for it yourself.)

## Initial State

### Google Sheets

The Google Sheet is reinitialized on each test; you can view the original data [here](https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/finalpool_dev/tasks/finalpool/gdp-cr5-analysis/preprocess).

```python 
# Let me extract the GDP data from the sheet in a more manageable way
import json

# First, let me get all the data from the Country sheet
from google_sheet import get_sheet_data

# Get the basic data structure
data = get_sheet_data("1QFN9EIvdUi5HEU9SsPSYVKqkpICHGQrF_xbKpdrwxTU", "Country")

# Extract just the values we need
countries = []
for i, row in enumerate(data['sheets'][0]['data'][0]['rowData']):
    if i == 0:  # Skip header
        continue
    
    if len(row.get('values', [])) >= 4:
        country_code = row['values'][0].get('effectiveValue', {}).get('stringValue', '')
        ranking = row['values'][1].get('effectiveValue', {}).get('numberValue', 0)
        country_name = row['values'][2].get('effectiveValue', {}).get('stringValue', '')
        gdp = row['values'][3].get('effectiveValue', {}).get('numberValue', 0)
        
        if country_code and country_name and gdp > 0:
            countries.append({
                'code': country_code,
                'ranking': int(ranking) if ranking else 0,
                'name': country_name,
                'gdp': gdp
            })

print(f"Found {len(countries)} countries with GDP data")
print("\nFirst 20 countries:")
for i, country in enumerate(countries[:20]):
    print(f"{country['ranking']:2d}. {country['name']:25s} {country['code']:3s} ${country['gdp']:,.0f}M")
```

```python 
import json
import requests

# Let me create a mapping of countries to regions based on World Bank classification
# I'll need to get all country data first, then group by regions

# First, let me extract the data I already have from the Region sheet
regions_data = {
    'EAS': {'name': 'East Asia & Pacific', 'total_gdp': 30655246.0302977},
    'ECS': {'name': 'Europe & Central Asia', 'total_gdp': 25192037.594848603},
    'LCN': {'name': 'Latin America & Caribbean', 'total_gdp': 6748778.26349321},
    'MEA': {'name': 'Middle East & North Africa', 'total_gdp': 4414423.06561728},
    'NAC': {'name': 'North America', 'total_gdp': 27610090.523673803},
    'SAS': {'name': 'South Asia', 'total_gdp': 4361631.45799902},
    'SSF': {'name': 'Sub-Saharan Africa', 'total_gdp': 2047347.01906553}
}

print("World Bank Regions and their total GDP:")
for code, data in regions_data.items():
    print(f"{code}: {data['name']} - ${data['total_gdp']:,.0f}M")
```

```python 
    'SDN': 'SSF', 'Sudan': 'SSF',
}

# Fix some misclassifications
country_to_region['TUN'] = 'MEA'  # Tunisia is MEA, not SSF
country_to_region['MLT'] = 'ECS'  # Malta is ECS

print("Country-to-region mapping created with", len(country_to_region), "entries")
print("\nSample mappings:")
for i, (country, region) in enumerate(list(country_to_region.items())[:10]):
    print(f"{country}: {region}")
```

```python 
# Group countries by region and calculate CR5 index
regions_data = {
    'EAS': {'name': 'East Asia & Pacific', 'total_gdp': 30655246.0302977},
    'ECS': {'name': 'Europe & Central Asia', 'total_gdp': 25192037.594848603},
    'LCN': {'name': 'Latin America & Caribbean', 'total_gdp': 6748778.26349321},
    'MEA': {'name': 'Middle East & North Africa', 'total_gdp': 4414423.06561728},
    'NAC': {'name': 'North America', 'total_gdp': 27610090.523673803},
    'SAS': {'name': 'South Asia', 'total_gdp': 4361631.45799902},
    'SSF': {'name': 'Sub-Saharan Africa', 'total_gdp': 2047347.01906553}
}

# Group countries by region
region_countries = {}
for region_code in regions_data.keys():
    region_countries[region_code] = []

# Assign countries to regions
for country in all_countries:
    country_key = country.get('code', country.get('name', ''))
    region = country_to_region.get(country_key) or country_to_region.get(country['name'])
    
    if region:
        country['region'] = region
        region_countries[region].append(country)
    else:
        print(f"Warning: No region found for {country['name']} ({country_key})")

# Calculate CR5 for each region
cr5_results = []

for region_code, region_info in regions_data.items():
    countries_in_region = region_countries[region_code]
    
    # Sort countries by GDP (descending)
    countries_in_region.sort(key=lambda x: x['gdp'], reverse=True)
    
    # Get top 5 countries
    top5_countries = countries_in_region[:5]
    top5_gdp_sum = sum(country['gdp'] for country in top5_countries)
    
    # Calculate CR5 ratio
    cr5_ratio = (top5_gdp_sum / region_info['total_gdp']) * 100
    
    # Prepare country names list
    top5_names = [country['name'] for country in top5_countries]
    
    cr5_results.append({
        'region': region_info['name'],
        'region_code': region_code,
        'top5_countries': ', '.join(top5_names),
        'top5_gdp_sum': top5_gdp_sum,
        'region_gdp_total': region_info['total_gdp'],
        'cr5_ratio': round(cr5_ratio, 2)
    })
    
    print(f"\n{region_code} - {region_info['name']}:")
    print(f"  Countries in region: {len(countries_in_region)}")
    print(f"  Top 5 countries: {', '.join(top5_names)}")
    print(f"  Top 5 GDP sum: ${top5_gdp_sum:,.0f}M")
    print(f"  Region total GDP: ${region_info['total_gdp']:,.0f}M")
    print(f"  CR5 ratio: {cr5_ratio:.2f}%")

# Sort results by CR5 ratio (descending)
cr5_results.sort(key=lambda x: x['cr5_ratio'], reverse=True)

print("\n" + "="*80)
print("CR5 ANALYSIS RESULTS (sorted by CR5 ratio descending):")
print("="*80)

for i, result in enumerate(cr5_results, 1):
    print(f"\n{i}. {result['region']} ({result['region_code']})")
    print(f"   CR5 Ratio: {result['cr5_ratio']}%")
    print(f"   Top 5: {result['top5_countries']}")
    print(f"   Top 5 GDP: ${result['top5_gdp_sum']:,.0f}M")
    print(f"   Total GDP: ${result['region_gdp_total']:,.0f}M")
```

```python 
# Group countries by region
region_countries = {}
for region_code in regions_data.keys():
    region_countries[region_code] = []

# Assign countries to regions
for country in all_countries:
    country_key = country.get('code', country.get('name', ''))
    region = country_to_region.get(country_key) or country_to_region.get(country['name'])
    
    if region:
        country['region'] = region
        region_countries[region].append(country)
    else:
        print(f"Warning: No region found for {country['name']} ({country_key})")

# Calculate CR5 for each region
cr5_results = []

for region_code, region_info in regions_data.items():
    countries_in_region = region_countries[region_code]
    
    # Sort countries by GDP (descending)
    countries_in_region.sort(key=lambda x: x['gdp'], reverse=True)
    
    # Get top 5 countries (or all if less than 5)
    top5_countries = countries_in_region[:5]
    top5_gdp_sum = sum(country['gdp'] for country in top5_countries)
    
    # Calculate CR5 ratio
    cr5_ratio = (top5_gdp_sum / region_info['total_gdp']) * 100
    
    # Prepare country names list
    top5_names = [country['name'] for country in top5_countries]
    
    cr5_results.append({
        'region': region_info['name'],
        'region_code': region_code,
        'top5_countries': ', '.join(top5_names),
        'top5_gdp_sum': top5_gdp_sum,
        'region_gdp_total': region_info['total_gdp'],
        'cr5_ratio': round(cr5_ratio, 2)
    })
    
    print(f"\n{region_code} - {region_info['name']}:")
    print(f"  Countries in region: {len(countries_in_region)}")
    if top5_countries:
        print(f"  Top 5 countries: {', '.join(top5_names)}")
        print(f"  Top 5 GDP sum: ${top5_gdp_sum:,.0f}M")
    else:
        print("  No countries found in this region from our dataset")
    print(f"  Region total GDP: ${region_info['total_gdp']:,.0f}M")
    if top5_countries:
        print(f"  CR5 ratio: {cr5_ratio:.2f}%")

# Sort results by CR5 ratio (descending)
cr5_results = [r for r in cr5_results if r['top5_gdp_sum'] > 0]  # Only include regions with data
cr5_results.sort(key=lambda x: x['cr5_ratio'], reverse=True)

print("\n" + "="*80)
print("CR5 ANALYSIS RESULTS (sorted by CR5 ratio descending):")
print("="*80)

for i, result in enumerate(cr5_results, 1):
    print(f"\n{i}. {result['region']} ({result['region_code']})")
    print(f"   CR5 Ratio: {result['cr5_ratio']}%")
    print(f"   Top 5: {result['top5_countries']}")
    print(f"   Top 5 GDP: ${result['top5_gdp_sum']:,.0f}M")
    print(f"   Total GDP: ${result['region_gdp_total']:,.0f}M")
```

```python 
    'CZE': 'ECS', 'Czech Republic': 'ECS',
    'UKR': 'ECS', 'Ukraine': 'ECS',
    'KAZ': 'ECS', 'Kazakhstan': 'ECS',
    
    # Latin America & Caribbean (LCN)

    'MEX': 'LCN', 'Mexico': 'LCN',

    # South Asia (SAS)

    # Middle East & North Africa (MEA)

# Regional totals from the spreadsheet
regions_data = {

    {'code': 'VNM', 'name': 'Vietnam', 'gdp': 408802, 'ranking': 37},
    {'code': 'SGP', 'name': 'Singapore', 'gdp': 396987, 'ranking': 38},
    {'code': 'PHL', 'name': 'Philippines', 'gdp': 394086, 'ranking': 39},
    {'code': 'DNK', 'name': 'Denmark', 'gdp': 390667, 'ranking': 40},
    {'code': 'COL', 'name': 'Colombia', 'gdp': 343622, 'ranking': 41},
    {'code': 'CHL', 'name': 'Chile', 'gdp': 317059, 'ranking': 42},
    {'code': 'FIN', 'name': 'Finland', 'gdp': 297301, 'ranking': 43},
    {'code': 'CZE', 'name': 'Czech Republic', 'gdp': 290774, 'ranking': 44},
    {'code': 'ROU', 'name': 'Romania', 'gdp': 284088, 'ranking': 45},
    {'code': 'IRQ', 'name': 'Iraq', 'gdp': 264182, 'ranking': 46},
    {'code': 'NZL', 'name': 'New Zealand', 'gdp': 249886, 'ranking': 47},
    {'code': 'PER', 'name': 'Peru', 'gdp': 242632, 'ranking': 48},
    {'code': 'KAZ', 'name': 'Kazakhstan', 'gdp': 220416, 'ranking': 49},
    {'code': 'UKR', 'name': 'Ukraine', 'gdp': 200086, 'ranking': 50},
]

# Group countries by region
region_countries = {}
for region_code in regions_data.keys():
    region_countries[region_code] = []

# Assign countries to regions
for country in all_countries:
    country_key = country.get('code', country.get('name', ''))
    region = country_to_region.get(country_key) or country_to_region.get(country['name'])
    
    if region:
        country['region'] = region
        region_countries[region].append(country)
    else:
        print(f"Warning: No region found for {country['name']} ({country_key})")

# Calculate CR5 for each region
cr5_results = []

print("REGIONAL ANALYSIS:")
print("="*60)

for region_code, region_info in regions_data.items():
    countries_in_region = region_countries[region_code]
    
    # Sort countries by GDP (descending)
    countries_in_region.sort(key=lambda x: x['gdp'], reverse=True)
    
    # Get top 5 countries (or all if less than 5)
    top5_countries = countries_in_region[:5]
    top5_gdp_sum = sum(country['gdp'] for country in top5_countries)
    
    # Calculate CR5 ratio
    if top5_gdp_sum > 0:
        cr5_ratio = (top5_gdp_sum / region_info['total_gdp']) * 100
    else:
        cr5_ratio = 0
    
    # Prepare country names list
    top5_names = [country['name'] for country in top5_countries]
    
    cr5_results.append({
        'region': region_info['name'],
        'region_code': region_code,
        'top5_countries': ', '.join(top5_names),
        'top5_gdp_sum': top5_gdp_sum,
        'region_gdp_total': region_info['total_gdp'],
        'cr5_ratio': round(cr5_ratio, 2)
    })
    
    print(f"\n{region_code} - {region_info['name']}:")
    print(f"  Countries in dataset: {len(countries_in_region)}")
    if top5_countries:
        print(f"  Top 5: {', '.join(top5_names)}")
        print(f"  Top 5 GDP: ${top5_gdp_sum:,.0f}M")
        print(f"  CR5 Ratio: {cr5_ratio:.2f}%")
    else:
        print("  No countries found in our dataset")
    print(f"  Total Regional GDP: ${region_info['total_gdp']:,.0f}M")

# Sort results by CR5 ratio (descending) and filter out empty regions
cr5_results = [r for r in cr5_results if r['top5_gdp_sum'] > 0]
cr5_results.sort(key=lambda x: x['cr5_ratio'], reverse=True)

print("\n" + "="*80)
print("FINAL CR5 ANALYSIS RESULTS (sorted by CR5 ratio descending):")
print("="*80)

final_results = []
for i, result in enumerate(cr5_results, 1):
    print(f"\n{i}. {result['region']} ({result['region_code']})")
    print(f"   CR5 Ratio: {result['cr5_ratio']}%")
    print(f"   Top 5: {result['top5_countries']}")
    print(f"   Top 5 GDP: ${result['top5_gdp_sum']:,.0f}M")
    print(f"   Total GDP: ${result['region_gdp_total']:,.0f}M")
    
    final_results.append([
        result['region'],
        result['top5_countries'],
        result['top5_gdp_sum'],
        result['region_gdp_total'],
        result['cr5_ratio']
    ])

print(f"\nProcessed {len(final_results)} regions with data")
```

```python 
# Prepare the data for the spreadsheet
final_data = [
    ["North America", "United States, Canada", 27602540, 27610090.523673803, 99.97],
    ["South Asia", "India, Bangladesh", 3845841, 4361631.45799902, 88.17],
    ["East Asia & Pacific", "China, Japan, Korea, Rep., Australia, Indonesia", 26999796, 30655246.0302977, 88.08],
    ["Latin America & Caribbean", "Brazil, Mexico, Argentina, Colombia, Chile", 4361042, 6748778.26349321, 64.62],
    ["Europe & Central Asia", "Germany, United Kingdom, France, Russian Federation, Italy", 14176619, 25192037.594848603, 56.27],
    ["Middle East & North Africa", "Saudi Arabia, United Arab Emirates, Egypt, Arab Rep., Iraq", 2074703, 4414423.06561728, 47.00],
    ["Sub-Saharan Africa", "Nigeria, South Africa", 859849, 2047347.01906553, 42.00]
]

print("Data to be inserted:")
print("Headers: Region, Top5_Countries, Top5_GDP_Sum, Region_GDP_Total, CR5_Ratio")
print()
for i, row in enumerate(final_data, 1):
    print(f"Row {i}: {row[0]}")
    print(f"  Top 5: {row[1]}")
    print(f"  Top 5 GDP: ${row[2]:,.0f}M")
    print(f"  Total GDP: ${row[3]:,.0f}M") 
    print(f"  CR5: {row[4]}%")
    print()

print(f"Total rows to insert: {len(final_data)}")
```

```python 
import json

# Load data from the saved overlong tool outputs
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/R7mWWZJaSGucF5kzBs7V4J.json', 'r') as f:
    country_data_str = json.load(f)["result"]["text"]
    country_data = json.loads(country_data_str)

with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/VqsAHYRKxiNHGzjkC3XDfi.json', 'r') as f:
    region_data_str = json.load(f)["result"]["text"]
    region_data = json.loads(region_data_str)

# World Bank regions
world_bank_regions = {
    "East Asia & Pacific": "EAS",
    "Europe & Central Asia": "ECS",
    "Latin America & Caribbean": "LCN",
    "Middle East & North Africa": "MEA",
    "North America": "NAC",
    "South Asia": "SAS",
    "Sub-Saharan Africa": "SSF"
}

# Extract country data
country_gdp = {}
country_to_region = {}

for row in country_data['sheets'][0]['data'][0]['rowData'][1:]:
    country_name = row['values'][2].get('effectiveValue', {}).get('stringValue')
    gdp = row['values'][3].get('effectiveValue', {}).get('numberValue')
    if country_name and gdp:
        country_gdp[country_name] = gdp

# Extract region data and total GDP
region_gdp_total = {}
for row in region_data['sheets'][0]['data'][0]['rowData'][1:]:
    region_name = row['values'][1].get('effectiveValue', {}).get('stringValue')
    gdp = row['values'][2].get('effectiveValue', {}).get('numberValue')
    if region_name and gdp and region_name in world_bank_regions:
        region_gdp_total[region_name] = gdp

# Manually create a mapping for some countries to regions as it is not in the sheet
country_to_region_manual = {
    'United States': 'North America',
    'China': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Japan': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Germany': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'India': 'South Asia',
    'United Kingdom': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'France': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Russian Federation': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Canada': 'North America',
    'Italy': 'Europe & Central Asia',

    'Mexico': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Spain': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Indonesia': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Saudi Arabia': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Netherlands': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Turkiye': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Switzerland': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Poland': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Argentina': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Sweden': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Ireland': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Belgium': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Norway': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Israel': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Thailand': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Austria': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Nigeria': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'United Arab Emirates': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Singapore': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Bangladesh': 'South Asia',
    'Egypt, Arab Rep.': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Vietnam': 'East Asia & Pacific',

    'Denmark': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Iran, Islamic Rep.': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Pakistan': 'South Asia',
    'Hong Kong SAR, China': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Colombia': 'Latin America & Caribbean',

    'Chile': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Czechia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Finland': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Portugal': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Peru': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'New Zealand': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Qatar': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Iraq': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Kazakhstan': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Greece': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Algeria': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Ukraine': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Kuwait': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Morocco': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Hungary': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Ethiopia': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Slovak Republic': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Kenya': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Oman': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Ecuador': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Dominican Republic': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Guatemala': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Angola': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Bulgaria': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Luxembourg': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Panama': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Costa Rica': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Tanzania': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Croatia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Uruguay': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Ghana': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Belarus': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Lithuania': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Cote d\'Ivoire': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Slovenia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Serbia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Azerbaijan': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Turkmenistan': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Uzbekistan': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Jordan': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Cameroon': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Bolivia': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Paraguay': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Uganda': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Bahrain': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Honduras': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Latvia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'El Salvador': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Estonia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Zimbabwe': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Nepal': 'South Asia',
    'Cyprus': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Georgia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Bosnia and Herzegovina': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Gabon': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Haiti': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Iceland': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Botswana': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Albania': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'North Macedonia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Malta': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Armenia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Moldova': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Montenegro': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Kosovo': 'Europe & Central Asia',
}

# Calculate CR5 for each region
cr5_results = []
for region_name, region_code in world_bank_regions.items():
    countries_in_region = {c: country_gdp[c] for c, r in country_to_region_manual.items() if r == region_name and c in country_gdp}
    
    if not countries_in_region:
        continue
        
    sorted_countries = sorted(countries_in_region.items(), key=lambda item: item[1], reverse=True)
    top5_countries = sorted_countries[:5]
    top5_names = [c[0] for c in top5_countries]
    top5_gdp_sum = sum(c[1] for c in top5_countries)
    
    total_gdp = region_gdp_total.get(region_name, 0)
    cr5_ratio = (top5_gdp_sum / total_gdp) * 100 if total_gdp else 0
    
    cr5_results.append([
        region_name,
        ", ".join(top5_names),
        top5_gdp_sum,
        total_gdp,
        f"{cr5_ratio:.2f}%"
    ])

# Sort results by CR5 ratio in descending order
sorted_cr5_results = sorted(cr5_results, key=lambda x: float(x[4][:-1]), reverse=True)

# Prepare data for Google Sheets
header = ["Region", "Top5_Countries", "Top5_GDP_Sum", "Region_GDP_Total", "CR5_Ratio"]
final_data = [header] + sorted_cr5_results

print(final_data)
```

```python 

import json

# Load data from the saved overlong tool outputs
with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/R7mWWZJaSGucF5kzBs7V4J.json', 'r') as f:
    tool_output = json.load(f)
    country_data_str = json.loads(tool_output['result'])['text']
    country_data = json.loads(country_data_str)

with open('/workspace/dumps/workspace/.overlong_tool_outputs/VqsAHYRKxiNHGzjkC3XDfi.json', 'r') as f:
    tool_output = json.load(f)
    region_data_str = json.loads(tool_output['result'])['text']
    region_data = json.loads(region_data_str)

# World Bank regions
world_bank_regions = {
    "East Asia & Pacific": "EAS",
    "Europe & Central Asia": "ECS",
    "Latin America & Caribbean": "LCN",
    "Middle East & North Africa": "MEA",
    "North America": "NAC",
    "South Asia": "SAS",
    "Sub-Saharan Africa": "SSF"
}

# Extract country data
country_gdp = {}
for row in country_data['sheets'][0]['data'][0]['rowData'][1:]:
    if len(row['values']) > 3:
        country_name = row['values'][2].get('effectiveValue', {}).get('stringValue')
        gdp = row['values'][3].get('effectiveValue', {}).get('numberValue')
        if country_name and gdp:
            country_gdp[country_name] = gdp

# Extract region data and total GDP
region_gdp_total = {}
for row in region_data['sheets'][0]['data'][0]['rowData'][1:]:
    if len(row['values']) > 2:
        region_name = row['values'][1].get('effectiveValue', {}).get('stringValue')
        gdp = row['values'][2].get('effectiveValue', {}).get('numberValue')
        if region_name and gdp and region_name in world_bank_regions:
            region_gdp_total[region_name] = gdp

# Manually create a mapping for some countries to regions as it is not in the sheet
country_to_region_manual = {
    'United States': 'North America',
    'China': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Japan': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Germany': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'India': 'South Asia',
    'United Kingdom': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'France': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Russian Federation': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Canada': 'North America',
    'Italy': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Brazil': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Australia': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Mexico': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Spain': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Indonesia': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Saudi Arabia': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Netherlands': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Turkiye': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Switzerland': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Poland': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Argentina': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Sweden': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Ireland': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Belgium': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Norway': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Israel': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Thailand': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Austria': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Nigeria': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'United Arab Emirates': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Singapore': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Bangladesh': 'South Asia',
    'Egypt, Arab Rep.': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Vietnam': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Malaysia': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'South Africa': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Philippines': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Denmark': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Iran, Islamic Rep.': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Pakistan': 'South Asia',
    'Hong Kong SAR, China': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Colombia': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Romania': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Chile': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Czechia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Finland': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Portugal': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Peru': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'New Zealand': 'East Asia & Pacific',
    'Qatar': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Iraq': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Kazakhstan': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Greece': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Algeria': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Ukraine': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Kuwait': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Morocco': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Hungary': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Ethiopia': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Slovak Republic': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Kenya': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Oman': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Ecuador': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Dominican Republic': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Guatemala': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Angola': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Bulgaria': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Luxembourg': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Panama': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Costa Rica': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Tanzania': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Croatia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Uruguay': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Ghana': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Belarus': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Lithuania': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Cote d\'Ivoire': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Slovenia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Serbia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Azerbaijan': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Turkmenistan': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Uzbekistan': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Jordan': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Cameroon': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Bolivia': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Paraguay': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Uganda': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Bahrain': 'Middle East & North Africa',
    'Honduras': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Latvia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'El Salvador': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Estonia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Zimbabwe': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Nepal': 'South Asia',
    'Cyprus': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Georgia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Bosnia and Herzegovina': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Gabon': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Haiti': 'Latin America & Caribbean',
    'Iceland': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Botswana': 'Sub-Saharan Africa',
    'Albania': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'North Macedonia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Malta': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Armenia': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Moldova': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Montenegro': 'Europe & Central Asia',
    'Kosovo': 'Europe & Central Asia',
}

# Calculate CR5 for each region
cr5_results = []
for region_name, region_code in world_bank_regions.items():
    countries_in_region = {c: country_gdp[c] for c, r in country_to_region_manual.items() if r == region_name and c in country_gdp}

    if not countries_in_region:
        continue

    sorted_countries = sorted(countries_in_region.items(), key=lambda item: item[1], reverse=True)
    top5_countries = sorted_countries[:5]
    top5_names = [c[0] for c in top5_countries]
    top5_gdp_sum = sum(c[1] for c in top5_countries)

    total_gdp = region_gdp_total.get(region_name, 0)
    cr5_ratio = (top5_gdp_sum / total_gdp) * 100 if total_gdp else 0

    cr5_results.append([
        region_name,
        ", ".join(top5_names),
        top5_gdp_sum,
        total_gdp,
        f"{cr5_ratio:.2f}%"
    ])

# Sort results by CR5 ratio in descending order
sorted_cr5_results = sorted(cr5_results, key=lambda x: float(x[4][:-1]), reverse=True)

# Prepare data for Google Sheets
header = ["Region", "Top5_Countries", "Top5_GDP_Sum", "Region_GDP_Total", "CR5_Ratio"]
final_data = [header] + sorted_cr5_results

print(json.dumps(final_data))
```
